<span data-ttu-id="1bb5f-1683">La classe **MS-DFSR-ContentSet** fait partie de la prise en charge du service de réplication système de fichiers DFS (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1bb5f-1683">The **ms-DFSR-ContentSet** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
